function addTestToUpaAbzTesting(upaAbtestingData, testName) {
upaAbtestingData = upaAbtestingData || '';
if (upaAbtestingData.length &gt; 0) {
upaAbtestingData += '|';
}
upaAbtestingData += testName;
var parameters = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 2);
while (parameters.length &gt; 0) {
upaAbtestingData += '|' + parameters[0] + '_' + parameters[1].replace(/_/g, '-');
parameters = parameters.slice(2);
}
return upaAbtestingData;
}

function addUrlParameters(url, parameters) {
for (var key in parameters) {
var value = parameters[key];
if (value != null) {
if (url.indexOf("=") &gt; 0) {
url += "&amp;";
}
url += key + "=" + value;
}
}
return url;
}
function fillSearchUrl(url, parametersOverride, stepIndex) {
if (url.indexOf("?") &lt; 0) {
url += '?';
}
var parameters = $.extend(true, {}, flightsOptions.searchQuery);
if (flightsOptions.stepsOptions != null &amp;&amp; stepIndex != null) {
parameters = $.extend(true, parameters, flightsOptions.stepsOptions[stepIndex]);
}
parameters = $.extend(true, parameters, parametersOverride);
url = addUrlParameters(url, parameters);
return url;
}
function loadCSS(href) {
var cssLink = $("&lt;link&gt;");
$("head").append(cssLink); //IE hack: append before setting href
cssLink.attr({
rel: "stylesheet",
type: "text/css",
href: href
});
};
</script>

var ajaxTimes = {};
function setAjaxTimes(result, final) {
if (ajaxTimes.firstClusterAjax == null) {
ajaxTimes.firstClusterAjax = new Date().getTime() - window.performance.timing.fetchStart;
}
if (final) {
ajaxTimes.allClustersAjax = new Date().getTime() - window.performance.timing.fetchStart;
}
if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.times != null) {
$.extend(result.times, ajaxTimes);
}
}
var sessionItem = window.sessionStorage.getItem("flights-gui");
if (sessionItem != null) {
var historyData = JSON.parse(sessionItem).history;
if (historyData != null &amp;&amp; historyData.searchQuery != null &amp;&amp; historyData.searchQuery.currency != null) {
flightsOptions.searchQuery.currency = historyData.searchQuery.currency;
}
}
ajaxTimes.beginAjax = new Date().getTime() - window.performance.timing.fetchStart;

// se espera que se inicialicen los modulos antes de lanzar los eventos
$.when(resultsInitializedDeferred).then(function() {
// si ya llego la respuesta final, se ignoran las partes
if (resultsDeferred.state() != "resolved") {
amplify.publish("doSearchStream", partialSearchResult);
resultsAjaxFinished = true;
}
});
});
streamedSearchAjax.on("final", function(finalSearchResult) {
setAjaxTimes(finalSearchResult, true);
resultsDeferred.resolve(finalSearchResult);
});
streamedSearchAjax.fail(function(error) {
resultsDeferred.reject("streaming-error");
console.log(error.thrown);
setTimeout(function() {throw error.thrown;}, 1);
});
</script>

<script async="">
amplify.subscribe("renderItemsFinished", function () {
var skeletonLoader = $('#skeleton-loader');
if(skeletonLoader.length &gt; 0){
skeletonLoader.remove();
$('.sbox-skeleton').remove();
$('.main-content, .results-research-container').addClass('-show');
setTimeout(function() {
$(".skeleton-component").remove();
}, 15000);
}
});
amplify.subscribe("showResultsErrorMessage", skeletonErrorHandler);
amplify.subscribe("noResults", skeletonErrorHandler);
function skeletonErrorHandler(){
var loader = $('#skeleton-loader');
if(loader.length &gt; 0) {
loader.remove();
$(".skeleton-component").remove();
$(".main-content, .results-research-container").addClass("-show");
}
}
</script>

var flightsSearchbox = {
init: function () {},
updateOrigin : function(cityCode, cityDescription, cityOid) {
amplify.publish("searchBox.setBoxModel", {
segment_1_origin_iata : cityCode
, segment_1_origin_code : cityCode
, segment_1_origin_description : cityDescription
});
}
, updateDestination : function(cityCode, cityDescription, cityOid) {
amplify.publish("searchBox.setBoxModel", {
segment_1_destination_iata : cityCode
, segment_1_destination_code : cityCode
, segment_1_destination_description : cityDescription
});
}
, updateMultipleOrigin : function(index, cityCode, cityDescription) {
var data = {};
data['segment_' + (index + 1) + '_origin_iata'] = cityCode;
data['segment_' + (index + 1) + '_origin_code'] = cityCode;
data['segment_' + (index + 1) + '_origin_description'] = cityDescription;
amplify.publish("searchBox.setBoxModel", data);
}
, updateMultipleDestination : function(index, cityCode, cityDescription) {
var data = {};
data['segment_' + (index + 1) + '_destination_iata'] = cityCode;
data['segment_' + (index + 1) + '_destination_code'] = cityCode;
data['segment_' + (index + 1) + '_destination_description'] = cityDescription;
amplify.publish("searchBox.setBoxModel", data);
}
, searchOverride : function(queries) {
if (queries !== undefined || queries !== ""){
amplify.publish("searchBox.searchOverride", queries);
}
}
, doSearch : function() {
amplify.publish("searchBox.doSearch");
}
};
mcReqJs.inject("flights", 'searchbox', function() {
return flightsSearchbox;
});

amplify.subscribe("searchBox.setBoxModel", function(newConfig) {
if (searchBox != null) {
searchBox.setBoxModel("flights", newConfig);
}
});
amplify.subscribe("searchBox.searchOverride", function(queries) {
if (searchBox != null) {
searchBox.searchOverride("flights",function(model, url){
var separator = (url.indexOf("?") &gt; 0) ? "&amp;" : "?";
window.location = url + separator + queries;
});
}
});
amplify.subscribe("searchBox.doSearch", function() {
if (searchBox != null) {
searchBox.trigger("flights:search");
}
});
amplify.subscribe("searchBox.lazyLoadStart", function() {
if (searchBox != null &amp;&amp; !alreadyLoad) {
searchBox.lazyLoad("flights").then(function () {
alreadyLoad = true;
searchBox.setInitBoxModel("flights", searchBoxInit);
}).done();
}
});
amplify.subscribe("searchBox.openResearch", function() {
if (searchBox &amp;&amp; alreadyLoad) {
//Prevent scroll under research modal
$('body').attr('style', 'height:100%;overflow:hidden;');
searchBox.show("flights", true);
}
$(".results-research-container").toggleClass("-show-content").promise().done( function() {
amplify.publish("searchBox.lazyLoadStart");
if ($(".results-research-container").hasClass("-show-content")) {
amplify.publish("researchExpanded")
}
});
if (searchBox &amp;&amp; alreadyLoad) {
searchBox.on("flights:onHide", function () {
$(".results-research-container").removeClass("-show-content")
//Enable scroll under research modal
$('body').attr('style', '');
});
}
});
amplify.subscribe("searchbox.updateStep", function(segment, type, data) {
var response = {};
response['segment_' + segment + '_' + type + '_code'] = data.code || "";
response['segment_' + segment + '_' + type + '_gid'] = data.gid || "";
response['segment_' + segment + '_' + type + '_iata'] = data.code || "";
response['segment_' + segment + '_' + type + '_description'] = data.name || "";
amplify.publish(((searchBox == null || !alreadyLoad) ? "searchBox.setAfterInit" : "searchBox.setBoxModel"), response);
});
amplify.subscribe("searchBox.setAfterInit", function(data) {
if (searchBoxInit != null &amp;&amp; searchBox == null) {
searchBoxInit = $.extend(true, searchBoxInit, data);
}
});
return [{
"boxes": {
"flights": {
"lazyload" : !alreadyLoad,
"config": {
"context": "search",
"flights+cars": true
},
"init": {}
}
}
, "callback": function (error, searchBoxInstance) {
if (!error) {
searchBox = searchBoxInstance;
}
}
}];
});
window.onload = function() {
amplify.publish("searchBox.lazyLoadStart");
};
